 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&#160;29, 2021, Domino&#8217;s Pizza, Inc. issued a press release announcing financial results for the first quarter ended March&#160;28, 2021. A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. The information in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and the Exhibit attached hereto are being furnished pursuant to Item 2.02 of Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and therefore shall not be deemed filed for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01. <TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Contact: Chris Brandon</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Director &#150; Investor Relations</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>(734) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">323-7932</FONT></B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U><B>Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Announces First Quarter 2021 Financial Results </B></U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Global retail sales growth (excluding foreign currency impact) of 14.0% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">U.S. same store sales growth of 13.4% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">International same store sales growth of 11.8% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Global net store growth of 175 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Diluted EPS down 2.3% to $3.00 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Completed recapitalization transaction in April 2021 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>ANN ARBOR, Michigan, April</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;29, 2021: Domino&#146;s Pizza, Inc. (NYSE: DPZ),</B> the largest pizza company in the world based on global
retail sales, announced results for the first quarter. Global retail sales increased 16.7% in the first quarter, or 14.0% excluding foreign currency impact. U.S. same store sales grew 13.4% during the quarter versus the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, continuing the positive sales momentum in the Company&#146;s U.S. stores business. The international business also posted strong results, with same store sales growth of 11.8% during the quarter.
The first quarter marked the 109<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of international same store sales growth and the 40<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of U.S. same
store sales growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company had first quarter global net store growth of 175 stores, comprised of 36 net U.S. store openings and 139 net
international store openings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First quarter diluted EPS was $3.00, down 2.3% over the prior year quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subsequent to the first quarter, on April&nbsp;27, 2021, the Company&#146;s Board of Directors declared a $0.94 per share quarterly dividend on its
outstanding common stock for shareholders of record as of June&nbsp;15, 2021, to be paid on June&nbsp;30, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;It was a strong first quarter for
the Domino&#146;s brand, with balanced growth across all areas of our global business,&#148; said Ritch Allison, Domino&#146;s Chief Executive Officer. &#147;I applaud our franchisees and operators all across the globe, who once again demonstrated
why they are the best in the restaurant business.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter Highlights (Unaudited): </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Revenues </B>increased $110.6&nbsp;million, or 12.7%, in the first quarter of 2021. This increase was
primarily due to U.S. and international same store sales growth and increases in global store counts during the trailing four quarters, resulting in higher supply chain, U.S. stores and international franchise revenues. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net Income</B> decreased $3.8&nbsp;million, or 3.2%, in the first quarter of 2021. This decrease was driven by
a significantly higher provision for income taxes resulting from lower tax benefits from equity-based compensation due to fewer stock option exercises in the first quarter of 2021 as compared to the first quarter of 2020. Income before provision
(benefit) for income taxes increased $32.3&nbsp;million in the first quarter of 2021 due to higher income from operations resulting from the increases in revenues described above. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted EPS</B> was $3.00 for the first quarter of 2021 versus $3.07 in the prior year quarter. This
represents a $0.07, or 2.3%, decrease from the prior year quarter. The decrease in diluted EPS was driven by lower net income and was partially offset by a lower weighted average diluted share count resulting from the Company&#146;s share
repurchases during the trailing four quarters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2021 Recapitalization </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subsequent to the end of the first quarter of 2021, on April&nbsp;16, 2021 (the &#147;closing date&#148;), the Company completed a previously announced
$1.85&nbsp;billion recapitalization transaction, including the issuance by certain of its subsidiaries of $850.0&nbsp;million of 2.662% fixed rate senior secured notes with an anticipated term of 7.5 years and $1.0&nbsp;billion of 3.151% fixed rate
senior secured notes with an anticipated term of 10 years (collectively, the &#147;2021 Notes&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company used a portion of the proceeds from the
recapitalization transaction to repay the remaining $291.0&nbsp;million in outstanding principal under its 2017 five-year floating rate notes and to repay the remaining $582.0&nbsp;million in outstanding principal under its 2017 five-year fixed rate
notes. The proceeds were also used to prefund a portion of the interest payable on the 2021 Notes and pay transaction fees and expenses. The Company expects to use the remaining proceeds for general corporate purposes, which may include
distributions to holders of the Company&#146;s common stock, other equivalent payments and/or stock repurchases. Certain of the Company&#146;s subsidiaries also issued a new $200.0&nbsp;million variable funding note facility, which was undrawn on
the closing date, and the Company&#146;s previous variable funding note facility was canceled. For additional information related to this recapitalization transaction, refer to the Company&#146;s Current Report on Form
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> filed on April&nbsp;20, 2021 and the Company&#146;s Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> for the quarter ended March&nbsp;28, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Comments on Regulation G </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to the GAAP
financial measures set forth in this press release, the Company has included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures within the meaning of Regulation G, including free cash flow metrics. The Company has also included
metrics such as global retail sales, global retail sales growth, global retail sales growth, excluding foreign currency impact and same store sales growth, which are commonly used statistical measures in the quick-service restaurant industry that
are important to understanding Company performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses &#147;<B>Global retail sales</B>&#148; to refer to total worldwide retail sales at
Company-owned and franchise stores. The Company believes global retail sales information is useful in analyzing revenues because franchisees pay royalties and advertising fees that are based on a percentage of franchise retail sales. The Company
reviews comparable industry global retail sales information to assess business trends and to track the growth of the Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> brand. In addition, supply chain revenues are directly
impacted by changes in franchise retail sales. Retail sales for franchise stores are reported to the Company by its franchisees and are not included in Company revenues. &#147;<B>Global retail sales growth</B>&#148; is calculated as the change of
U.S.&nbsp;Dollar global retail sales against the comparable period of the prior year. &#147;<B>Global retail sales growth, excluding foreign currency impact</B>&#148; is calculated as the change of international local currency global retail sales
against the comparable period of the prior year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses &#147;<B>Same store sales growth</B>,&#148; which is calculated by including only sales
from stores that also had sales in the comparable weeks of both years. International same store sales growth is calculated similarly to U.S. same store sales growth. Changes in international same store sales are reported excluding foreign currency
impacts, which reflect changes in international local currency sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses <B>&#147;Free cash flow,&#148;</B> which is calculated as net cash
provided by operating activities, less capital expenditures, both as reported under GAAP. The Company believes that the free cash flow measure is important to investors and other interested persons, and that such persons benefit from having a
measure which communicates how much cash flow is available for working capital needs or to be used for repurchasing debt, making acquisitions, repurchasing common stock or paying dividends. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Founded in 1960, Domino&#146;s Pizza is the largest pizza company in the world based on retail sales, with a significant business in both delivery and carryout
pizza. It ranks among the world&#146;s top public restaurant brands with a global enterprise of more than 17,800 stores in over 90 markets. Domino&#146;s had global retail sales of over $16.1&nbsp;billion in 2020, with nearly $8.3&nbsp;billion in
the U.S. and over $7.8&nbsp;billion internationally. In the first quarter of 2021, Domino&#146;s had global retail sales of over $4.0&nbsp;billion, with nearly $2.0&nbsp;billion in the U.S. and over $2.0&nbsp;billion internationally. Its system is
comprised of independent franchise owners who accounted for 98% of Domino&#146;s stores as of the end of the first quarter of 2021. Emphasis on technology innovation helped Domino&#146;s achieve more than half of all global retail sales in 2020 from
digital channels. In the U.S., Domino&#146;s generated more than 70% of sales in 2020 via digital channels and has developed several innovative ordering platforms, including those for Google Home, Facebook Messenger, Apple Watch, Amazon Echo,
Twitter and more. In 2019, Domino&#146;s announced a partnership with Nuro to further its exploration and testing of autonomous pizza delivery. In <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-2020,</FONT> Domino&#146;s launched a new way to order
contactless carryout nationwide &#150; via Domino&#146;s Carside Delivery<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, which customers can choose when placing a prepaid online order. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Order &#150; <U>dominos.com</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Company Info &#150;
<U>biz.dominos.com</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Media Assets &#150; <U>media.dominos.com</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Please visit our Investor Relations website at biz.dominos.com to view news, announcements, earnings releases, investor presentations and conference webcasts.
</P>
